Duke:\n\nStoicism ek ancient Greek philosophy hai — Zeno of Citium ne start ki thi, aur baad mein Seneca, Epictetus, Marcus Aurelius jaise logo ne develop ki.\n\n──\n\n**Core idea:**\nTumhare control mein sirf tumhare thoughts, actions aur reactions hain. Bahar ki duniya — logo ka behavior, events, outcomes — tumhare control mein nahi hai. Peace tab milti hai jab tum sirf apne control wali chize pe focus karte ho.\n\n**Key principles:**\n• **Dichotomy of control** — differentiate karo kya tumhare hath mein hai, kya nahi\n• **Virtue over pleasure** — wisdom, courage, justice, discipline ye asli success hai, na ki fame/money\n• **Amor fati** — jo bhi ho raha hai usse accept karo, fight mat karo reality se\n• **Memento mori** — life short hai, isliye distractions mein waste mat karo\n\n──\n\n✨ Bonus: Marcus Aurelius Roman emperor tha, aur uski personal diary \"Meditations\" aaj tak best self-help books mein count hoti hai — usne kabhi publish karne ke liye likha bhi nahi tha.\n\nKya specifically interest hai — philosophy ka background, ya practical application (jaise stress/procrastination handle karne
